    Switch -->|CONNECTED_CAR| TransCC[Return translated 'Connected Car']
    Switch -->|ORIGIN_AND_DESTINATION| TransOD[Return translated 'Origin & Destination']
    Switch -->|MILESTONES| TransM[Return translated 'Milestones']
    Switch -->|SHIPMENT_COORDINATES| TransSC[Return translated 'Shipment Coordinates']
    Switch -->|default| LogWarn[Log warning for missing translation]
    LogWarn --> ReturnOrig[Return original option]
    TransCC --> CallEnd([End])
    TransOD --> CallEnd
    TransM --> CallEnd
    TransSC --> CallEnd
    ReturnOrig --> CallEnd

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Component
    participant Hook as useMapPreferenceOptionsTranslation
    participant i18n as useTranslation
    participant Logger as logWarningForMissingTranslation
    
    Component->>Hook: Call hook
    Hook->>i18n: useTranslation('component')
    i18n-->>Hook: Return t function
    Hook-->>Component: Return {getTranslatedOption}
    
    Component->>Hook: getTranslatedOption(option)
    alt option is MapPreference constant
        Hook->>i18n: t(translation_key)
        i18n-->>Hook: Translated string
        Hook-->>Component: Translated string
    else option is unknown
        Hook->>Logger: logWarningForMissingTranslation(option)
        Hook-->>Component: Original option
    end
```
